[30;1m91 | [0m[35mA configuration object is little more than a wrapper around a dictionary.[0m
[30;1m92 | [0m[35mA configuration *file* is simply a mechanism for producing that object.[0m

[30;1m94 | [0m[35mThe former has the benefit that it can perform extensive logic to populate[0m
